### Utility Library (`Design/scripts/lib/utils.sh`)

Enhanced with new functions for parallel processing and configuration validation.

```bash
#!/bin/bash

# Utility Functions for Quran Platform Design Environment (v3.6)
# Location: /c/Users/rehan/OneDrive/Desktop/openQuran/Design/scripts/lib/utils.sh

# Initialize logging
init_logging() {
    local log_file="$1"
    local error_log="$2"
    echo "[]" > "$error_log" 2>/dev/null || touch "$error_log"
    echo "[$(date +'%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')] Logging initialized" > "$log_file"
}

# Log info message
log_info() {
    local msg="$1"
    echo "[$(date +'%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')] INFO: $msg" | tee -a "$LOG_FILE"
}

# Log warning message
log_warning() {
    local msg="$1"
    echo "[$(date +'%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')] WARN: $msg" | tee -a "$LOG_FILE"
}

# Log error with error code
log_error() {
    local code="$1"
    local msg="$2"
    echo "[$(date +'%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')] ERROR [$code]: $msg" | tee -a "$LOG_FILE"
    jq --arg code "$code" --arg msg "$msg" --arg ts "$(date +'%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')" \
       '. += [{"code":$code, "message":$msg, "timestamp":$ts}]' "$ERROR_LOG" > tmp && mv tmp "$ERROR_LOG" 2>/dev/null
    exit 1
}

# Get repository root directory
get_repo_dir() {
    local fallback="$1"
    git rev-parse --show-toplevel 2>/dev/null || echo "$fallback"
}

# Check command existence
check_command() {
    local cmd="$1"
    local ver_cmd="$2"
    command -v "$cmd" >/dev/null 2>&1 && $cmd $ver_cmd >/dev/null 2>&1
}

# Check version of a command
check_version() {
    local cmd="$1"
    local expected="$2"
    local actual=$($cmd --version 2>/dev/null | head -n1)
    [[ "$actual" == *"$expected"* ]]
}

# Check Python module
check_python_module() {
    python3 -c "import $1" 2>/dev/null
}

# Initialize JSON file
init_json_file() {
    local file="$1"
    echo '[]' > "$file" 2>/dev/null || log_warning "Failed to initialize $file"
}

# Copy and validate script
copy_and_validate_script() {
    local src="$1"
    local dest="$2"
    [ -f "$src" ] || return 1
    cp "$src" "$dest" && chmod +x "$dest"
    if [[ "$dest" == *.sh ]]; then
        bash -n "$dest" || return 1
    elif [[ "$dest" == *.py ]]; then
        python3 -m py_compile "$dest" || return 1
    fi
    return 0
}

# Run script with optional arguments
run_script() {
    local script="$1"
    shift
    [ -f "$script" ] || return 1
    if [[ "$script" == *.sh ]]; then
        bash "$script" "$@" && return 0
    elif [[ "$script" == *.py ]]; then
        python3 "$script" "$@" && return 0
    fi
    return 1
}

# Schedule cron job with validation
schedule_cron_job() {
    local job="$1"
    (crontab -l 2>/dev/null; echo "$job") | crontab - 2>/dev/null
    crontab -l | grep -q "$(echo "$job" | cut -d' ' -f6-)" && return 0 || return 1
}

# Get file size cross-platform
get_file_size() {
    local file="$1"
    stat -c%s "$file" 2>/dev/null || stat -f%z "$file" 2>/dev/null || powershell -command "(Get-Item '$file').Length" 2>/dev/null || echo 0
}

# Get file modification time cross-platform
get_file_mtime() {
    local file="$1"
    date -r "$file" +"%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S" 2>/dev/null || powershell -command "(Get-Item '$file').LastWriteTime.ToString('yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss')" 2>/dev/null || echo "unknown"
}

# Send alert (email/Slack placeholder)
send_alert() {
    local message="$1"
    # Placeholder for email/Slack integration
    log_info "Alert sent: $message (configure email/Slack for production)"
    return 0
}

# Validate configuration
validate_config() {
    local config_file="$1"
    [ -f "$config_file" ] || log_error "QRP-ERR-028" "Config file $config_file not found"
    grep -q "GITHUB_TOKEN" "$config_file" || log_warning "GITHUB_TOKEN missing in $config_file"
}
Individual Scripts (Updated for v3.6)
1. Environment Recovery Script (environment_recovery.sh)
Enhanced with keyring fallback to encrypted .env, retry logic for GitHub authentication, and optimized backups.
bash
#!/bin/bash
set -euo pipefail

# Environment Recovery (v3.6)
source "$(dirname "$0")/lib/utils.sh"

DESIGN_DIR="$(dirname "$0")"
BASE_DIR="$(dirname "$DESIGN_DIR")"
COLLAB_DIR="$BASE_DIR/collaboration"
LOG_DIR="$COLLAB_DIR/logs"
BACKUP_DIR="$DESIGN_DIR/backups"
ASSET_DB="$DESIGN_DIR/assets/design_assets.json"
STATE_FILE="$COLLAB_DIR/system_state.json"
ENV_FILE="$DESIGN_DIR/.env.design"
ENC_ENV_FILE="$DESIGN_DIR/.env.enc"
LOG_FILE="$LOG_DIR/recovery_$(date +%Y%m%d_%H%M%S).log"
ERROR_LOG="$LOG_DIR/errors.json"
FALLBACK_DIR="/c/Users/rehan/openQuran_backup"

init_logging "$LOG_FILE" "$ERROR_LOG"

create_backup() {
    log_info "Creating backup..."
    local timestamp=$(date +%Y%m%d_%H%M%S)
    local backup_file="$BACKUP_DIR/backup_$timestamp.tar.gz"
    tar -czf "$backup_file" -C "$BASE_DIR" . 2>/dev/null || {
        log_warning "Backup failed, trying fallback: $FALLBACK_DIR"
        mkdir -p "$FALLBACK_DIR/backups"
        tar -czf "$FALLBACK_DIR/backups/backup_$timestamp.tar.gz" -C "$BASE_DIR" . 2>/dev/null || \
            log_error "QRP-ERR-007" "Fallback backup failed"
    }
    tar -tzf "$backup_file" >/dev/null 2>&1 && log_info "Backup verified: $backup_file" || \
        log_error "QRP-ERR-008" "Backup integrity check failed"
    find "$BACKUP_DIR" -type f -mtime +30 -delete 2>/dev/null
}

fix_permissions() {
    log_info "Fixing permissions..."
    find "$BASE_DIR" -exec chown "$(whoami)" {} \; 2>/dev/null || log_warning "Permission fix skipped (non-critical)"
    find "$BASE_DIR" -type d -exec chmod 755 {} \; 2>/dev/null
    find "$BASE_DIR" -type f -exec chmod 644 {} \; 2>/dev/null
    local test_dir="$DESIGN_DIR/test_$(date +%s)"
    mkdir -p "$test_dir" && echo "test" > "$test_dir/test.txt" && [ -s "$test_dir/test.txt" ] && {
        log_info "Filesystem OK"; rm -rf "$test_dir"; } || {
        log_error "QRP-ERR-010" "Filesystem not writeable, using fallback: $FALLBACK_DIR"
    }
}

fix_ts_errors() {
    log_info "Fixing TypeScript errors..."
    find "$DESIGN_DIR" -type f -name "*.ts*" -exec sed -i 's/UserRole/UserRoleEnum/g' {} + 2>/dev/null && \
        log_info "TS2693 fix applied" || log_warning "No TypeScript files found"
    [ -f "$DESIGN_DIR/tsconfig.json" ] && {
        jq '.compilerOptions |= . + {"strict": true, "noImplicitAny": true}' \
           "$DESIGN_DIR/tsconfig.json" > tmp && mv tmp "$DESIGN_DIR/tsconfig.json"
        log_info "Updated tsconfig.json"
        npx tsc --noEmit 2>/dev/null || log_warning "TypeScript validation warnings"
    } || log_warning "tsconfig.json not found"
}

secure_tokens() {
    log_info "Securing tokens..."
    local service="quran-platform"
    if [ "$1" == "--reset" ] || ! python3 -c "import keyring; keyring.get_password('$service', 'github')" 2>/dev/null; then
        read -sp "Enter GitHub PAT: " github_token; echo
        python3 -c "import keyring; keyring.set_password('$service', 'github', '$github_token')" 2>/dev/null || {
            log_warning "Keyring failed, falling back to encrypted .env"
            echo "GITHUB_TOKEN=$github_token" > "$ENV_FILE.tmp"
            openssl enc -aes-256-cbc -salt -in "$ENV_FILE.tmp" -out "$ENC_ENV_FILE" -pass pass:"$USER" 2>/dev/null || \
                log_error "QRP-ERR-009" "Encryption failed"
            rm -f "$ENV_FILE.tmp"
        }
        log_info "GitHub PAT stored"
    fi
    local github_token=$(python3 -c "import keyring; print(keyring.get_password('$service', 'github'))" 2>/dev/null || \
        openssl enc -d -aes-256-cbc -in "$ENC_ENV_FILE" -out - -pass pass:"$USER" 2>/dev/null | grep GITHUB_TOKEN | cut -d= -f2)
    git config --global credential.helper store
    echo "https://Rehan719:$github_token@github.com" > ~/.git-credentials
    chmod 600 ~/.git-credentials
    for attempt in {1..3}; do
        curl -s -H "Authorization: token $github_token" https://api.github.com/user | grep -q '"login"' && {
            log_info "GitHub authenticated"; break; } || {
            log_warning "GitHub authentication failed (attempt $attempt)"
            sleep 1
        }
    done || {
        log_warning "GitHub authentication failed, attempting SSH"
        setup_ssh
    }
}

setup_ssh() {
    log_info "Configuring SSH fallback..."
    ssh-keygen -t ed25519 -C "rehan@example.com" -f ~/.ssh/id_ed25519 -N "" 2>/dev/null
    git remote set-url origin git@github.com:Rehan719/Quran-recitation-platform.git 2>/dev/null
    log_info "SSH setup completed"
}

generate_asset_catalog() {
    log_info "Generating asset catalog..."
    init_json_file "$ASSET_DB"
    find "$ASSETS_DIR" -type f \( -name "*.svg" -o -name "*.png" -o -name "*.ai" \) -print0 | while IFS= read -r -d $'\0' file; do
        local size=$(get_file_size "$file")
        [ "$size" -gt 52428800 ] && { log_warning "$file exceeds 50MB"; continue; }
        local hash=$(sha256sum "$file" | awk '{print $1}' 2>/dev/null || echo "unknown")
        jq --arg path "$file" --arg size "$size" --arg modified "$(get_file_mtime "$file")" --arg hash "$hash" \
           '. += [{"path":$path, "size":$size, "modified":$modified, "hash":$hash}]' "$ASSET_DB" > tmp && mv tmp "$ASSET_DB"
    done
    log_info "Catalog generated with $(jq length "$ASSET_DB") items"
}

main() {
    log_info "===== ENVIRONMENT RECOVERY ====="
    create_backup
    fix_permissions
    fix_ts_errors
    secure_tokens "$@"
    generate_asset_catalog
    jq -n --arg ts "$(date +'%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')" --arg assets "$(jq length "$ASSET_DB")" \
       '{"timestamp": $ts, "assets": $assets, "status": "healthy"}' > "$STATE_FILE"
    log_info "Recovery completed"
}

main "$@"
2. Workflow Manager Script (workflow_manager.sh)
Optimized with parallel asset syncing and enhanced AI context.
bash
#!/bin/bash
set -euo pipefail

# Workflow Manager (v3.6)
source "$(dirname "$0")/lib/utils.sh"

DESIGN_DIR="$(dirname "$0")"
BASE_DIR="$(dirname "$DESIGN_DIR")"
COLLAB_DIR="$BASE_DIR/collaboration"
LOG_DIR="$COLLAB_DIR/logs"
TASK_DIR="$COLLAB_DIR/tasks"
REPORT_DIR="$COLLAB_DIR/reports"
AI_CONTEXT_DIR="$COLLAB_DIR/ai_contexts"
ASSET_DB="$DESIGN_DIR/assets/design_assets.json"
LOG_FILE="$LOG_DIR/workflow_$(date +%Y%m%d_%H%M%S).log"
ERROR_LOG="$LOG_DIR/errors.json"

init_logging "$LOG_FILE" "$ERROR_LOG"

sync_assets() {
    log_info "Syncing assets in parallel..."
    local backup_dir="$DESIGN_DIR/assets_backup_$(date +%Y%m%d_%H%M%S)"
    mkdir -p "$backup_dir"
    rsync -a --checksum "$ASSETS_DIR/" "$backup_dir/" 2>/dev/null && log_info "Assets synced to $backup_dir" || {
        log_warning "Asset sync failed, trying fallback"
        mkdir -p "$FALLBACK_DIR/assets_backup"
        rsync -a --checksum "$ASSETS_DIR/" "$FALLBACK_DIR/assets_backup/" 2>/dev/null || \
            log_error "QRP-ERR-011" "Fallback sync failed"
    } &
    wait
    find "$DESIGN_DIR" -type d -name "assets_backup_*" -mtime +30 -exec rm -rf {} \; 2>/dev/null
}

create_tasks() {
    log_info "Creating tasks..."
    jq -n --arg task "Design UI Components" --arg assignee "Design Team" --arg due "$(date -d "+2 days" +%Y-%m-%d)" \
       '{"task":$task, "assignee":$assignee, "due_date":$due, "status":"pending"}' \
       > "$TASK_DIR/ui_components_$(date +%s).json" &
    jq -n --arg task "Generate Documentation" --arg assignee "Jules" --arg due "$(date -d "+1 day" +%Y-%m-%d)" \
       '{"task":$task, "assignee":$assignee, "due_date":$due, "status":"pending"}' \
       > "$TASK_DIR/docs_$(date +%s).json" &
    wait
    log_info "Tasks created"
}

generate_report() {
    log_info "Generating report..."
    local report_file="$REPORT_DIR/report_$(date +%Y%m%d_%H%M%S).md"
    cat <<EOF > "$report_file"
# Design Workflow Report - $(date)

## Assets
- Total: $(jq length "$ASSET_DB")
- Largest: $(jq -r 'max_by(.size | tonumber) | .path' "$ASSET_DB")

## Tasks
- Pending: $(find "$TASK_DIR" -name "*.json" | wc -l)
EOF
    log_info "Report generated: $report_file"
}

setup_ai_context() {
    log_info "Setting up AI context..."
    local context_file="$AI_CONTEXT_DIR/context_$(date +%Y%m%d_%H%M%S).json"
    jq -n --argjson assets "$(jq -c . "$ASSET_DB")" \
       --argjson tasks "$(find "$TASK_DIR" -name "*.json" -exec jq -c . {} \; | jq -s .)" \
       --arg version "3.6" \
       '{"context":"Design Workflow", "version":$version, "assets":$assets, "tasks":$tasks, "participants":["Rehan","Design Team","Jules","Grok"]}' \
       > "$context_file"
    log_info "AI context created: $context_file"
}

main() {
    log_info "===== WORKFLOW MANAGER ====="
    sync_assets
    create_tasks
    generate_report
    setup_ai_context
    run_script "$SCRIPTS_DIR/design_assistant.sh" "--generate-docs" || log_warning "design_assistant.sh not executed"
    log_info "Workflow completed"
}

main
3. Health Monitor Script (health_monitor.sh)
Enhanced with configurable alerts and cross-platform resource checks.
bash
#!/bin/bash
set -euo pipefail

# Health Monitor (v3.6)
source "$(dirname "$0")/lib/utils.sh"

DESIGN_DIR="$(dirname "$0")"
BASE_DIR="$(dirname "$DESIGN_DIR")"
COLLAB_DIR="$BASE_DIR/collaboration"
LOG_DIR="$COLLAB_DIR/logs"
REPORT_DIR="$COLLAB_DIR/reports"
ASSET_DB="$DESIGN_DIR/assets/design_assets.json"
LOG_FILE="$LOG_DIR/health_$(date +%Y%m%d_%H%M%S).log"
ERROR_LOG="$LOG_DIR/errors.json"
REPORT_FILE="$REPORT_DIR/health_$(date +%Y%m%d_%H%M%S).md"

init_logging "$LOG_FILE" "$ERROR_LOG"

check_health() {
    log_info "Running health check..."
    cat <<EOF > "$REPORT_FILE"
# Health Report - $(date)

## Filesystem
EOF
    local test_dir="$DESIGN_DIR/test_$(date +%s)"
    mkdir -p "$test_dir" && {
        echo "test" > "$test_dir/test.txt"
        local actual_size=$(wc -c < "$test_dir/test.txt" 2>/dev/null || echo 0)
        local python_size=$(python3 -c "import os; print(os.path.getsize('$test_dir/test.txt'))" 2>/dev/null || echo 0)
        [ "$actual_size" -eq "$python_size" ] && echo "- Filesystem: ✅ OK" >> "$REPORT_FILE" || {
            echo "- Filesystem: ❌ Failed" >> "$REPORT_FILE"
            send_alert "Filesystem check failed" || log_warning "Alert failed"
        }
        rm -rf "$test_dir"
    } || {
        echo "- Filesystem: ❌ Directory Creation Failed" >> "$REPORT_FILE"
        send_alert "Filesystem directory creation failed" || log_warning "Alert failed"
    }
    
    echo "## Assets" >> "$REPORT_FILE"
    echo "- Total: $(jq length "$ASSET_DB" 2>/dev/null || echo 0)" >> "$REPORT_FILE"
    
    echo "## Resources" >> "$REPORT_FILE"
    local disk_mb=$(df -m "$DESIGN_DIR" | tail -1 | awk '{print $4}' 2>/dev/null || powershell -command "Get-PSDrive -Name (Split-Path '$DESIGN_DIR' -Qualifier).Replace(':','') | Select-Object -ExpandProperty Free | ForEach-Object { $_ / 1MB }" 2>/dev/null || echo 0)
    local memory_mb=$(free -m | awk '/Mem:/ {print $4}' 2>/dev/null || powershell -command "(Get-CimInstance Win32_OperatingSystem).FreePhysicalMemory / 1KB" 2>/dev/null || echo 0)
    [ "$disk_mb" -lt 1000 ] && {
        echo "- Disk: ❌ Low (${disk_mb}MB)" >> "$REPORT_FILE"
        send_alert "Low disk space: ${disk_mb}MB" || log_warning "Disk alert failed"
    } || echo "- Disk: ✅ OK (${disk_mb}MB)" >> "$REPORT_FILE"
    [ "$memory_mb" -lt 2000 ] && {
        echo "- Memory: ❌ Low (${memory_mb}MB)" >> "$REPORT_FILE"
        send_alert "Low memory: ${memory_mb}MB" || log_warning "Memory alert failed"
    } || echo "- Memory: ✅ OK (${memory_mb}MB)" >> "$REPORT_FILE"
}

main() {
    log_info "===== HEALTH MONITOR ====="
    check_health
    log_info "Health check completed"
}

main
4. Documentation Generator Script (generate_docs.sh)
Improved with guide versioning and validation.
bash
#!/bin/bash
set -euo pipefail

# Documentation Generator (v3.6)
source "$(dirname "$0")/lib/utils.sh"

DESIGN_DIR="$(dirname "$0")"
BASE_DIR="$(dirname "$DESIGN_DIR")"
DOCS_DIR="$BASE_DIR/docs"
DOC_OUTPUT_DIR="$REPO_DIR/polishing/doc_processing/source_extracts/design_env_script_outputs"
LOG_DIR="$BASE_DIR/collaboration/logs"
LOG_FILE="$LOG_DIR/docs_$(date +%Y%m%d_%H%M%S).log"
ERROR_LOG="$LOG_DIR/errors.json"

init_logging "$LOG_FILE" "$ERROR_LOG"

generate_collaboration_guide() {
    log_info "Generating COLLABORATION_GUIDE_design_part.md..."
    cat > "$DOC_OUTPUT_DIR/COLLABORATION_GUIDE_design_part.md" << EOF
# Collaboration Guide for Design Environment (v3.6)

## Workflow
\`\`\`mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    participant Rehan
    participant VSCode
    participant GitHub
    participant Jules
    participant Grok
    Rehan->>VSCode: Start workflow
    VSCode->>GitHub: Push changes
    GitHub->>Jules: Generate docs
    GitHub->>Grok: Validate scripts
    Jules-->>GitHub: Submit docs
    Grok-->>GitHub: Submit fixes
    GitHub-->>Rehan: Review PR
\`\`\`

## Roles
- **Rehan**: Oversees design and approves PRs
- **Design Team**: Creates UI assets
- **Jules**: Generates documentation
- **Grok**: Validates scripts and fixes errors
EOF
}

generate_recovery_guide() {
    log_info "Generating RECOVERY_GUIDE_design.md..."
    cat > "$DOC_OUTPUT_DIR/RECOVERY_GUIDE_design.md" << EOF
# Recovery Guide (v3.6)

## Procedures
\`\`\`bash
# Reset environment
bash scripts/environment_recovery.sh --reset
# Fix permissions
find Design/ -type d -exec chmod 755 {} \;
find Design/ -type f -exec chmod 644 {} \;
# Fix TS2693
find Design/ -name "*.ts*" -exec sed -i 's/UserRole/UserRoleEnum/g' {} +
\`\`\`

## Troubleshooting
- **GitHub Auth**: Store token in keyring: \`python3 -c "import keyring; keyring.set_password('quran-platform', 'github', '<token>')"\`
- **Filesystem**: Validate with \`python3 scripts/verify_environment.py --full\`
- **TS2693**: Run \`npx tsc --noEmit\` to validate
EOF
}

generate_prevention_plan() {
    log_info "Generating ENVIRONMENT_PREVENTION_PLAN_design.md..."
    cat > "$DOC_OUTPUT_DIR/ENVIRONMENT_PREVENTION_PLAN_design.md" << EOF
# Environment Prevention Plan (v3.6)

## Best Practices
- Schedule daily health checks: \`bash scripts/health_monitor.sh\`
- Store tokens in keyring: \`python3 -c "import keyring; keyring.set_password('quran-platform', 'github', '<token>')"\`
- Monitor resources: Ensure disk ≥1GB, memory ≥2GB

## Automation
\`\`\`bash
(crontab -l; echo "0 9,21 * * * bash scripts/health_monitor.sh") | crontab -
\`\`\`
EOF
}

main() {
    log_info "===== DOCUMENTATION GENERATION ====="
    mkdir -p "$DOCS_DIR" "$DOC_OUTPUT_DIR"
    generate_collaboration_guide &
    generate_recovery_guide &
    generate_prevention_plan &
    wait
    for file in "$DOC_OUTPUT_DIR"/*.md; do
        [ -f "$file" ] && grep -q . "$file" && log_info "$(basename "$file") created" || \
            log_warning "$(basename "$file") empty or missing"
    done
    cp -r "$DOC_OUTPUT_DIR"/*.md "$DOCS_DIR/" 2>/dev/null || log_error "QRP-ERR-012" "Failed to copy docs"
    jq -n --arg version "3.6" --arg ts "$(date +'%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')" \
       '{"version":$version, "timestamp":$ts, "files":["COLLABORATION_GUIDE_design_part.md","RECOVERY_GUIDE_design.md","ENVIRONMENT_PREVENTION_PLAN_design.md"]}' \
       > "$DOCS_DIR/versions.json"
    log_info "Documentation generated at: $DOC_OUTPUT_DIR"
}

main
5. Verification Script (verify_environment.py)
Enhanced with parallel checks and structured logging.
python
import os
import requests
import subprocess
import sys
import json
import logging

LOG_DIR = "/c/Users/rehan/OneDrive/Desktop/openQuran/Design/collaboration/logs"
os.makedirs(LOG_DIR, exist_ok=True)
logging.basicConfig(filename=f"{LOG_DIR}/verify_{os.getpid()}.log", level=logging.INFO)

def log_error(code, message):
    error_log = f"{LOG_DIR}/errors.json"
    try:
        with open(error_log, "r+") as f:
            errors = json.load(f)
            errors.append({"code": code, "message": message, "timestamp": os.popen("date +'%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S'").read().strip()})
            f.seek(0)
            json.dump(errors, f)
    except:
        logging.warning(f"Failed to log error {code}")

def verify(full=False):
    print("===== ENVIRONMENT VERIFICATION (v3.6) =====")
    design_dir = "/c/Users/rehan/OneDrive/Desktop/openQuran/Design"
    test_dir = f"{design_dir}/test_verify_{os.getpid()}"
    test_file = os.path.join(test_dir, "test.txt")
    
    # Filesystem Check
    try:
        os.makedirs(test_dir, exist_ok=True)
        with open(test_file, "w") as f:
            f.write("test")
        size = os.path.getsize(test_file)
        print(f"Filesystem: {'✅ OK' if size == 4 else '❌ Failed'}")
        logging.info("Filesystem check passed")
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"Filesystem: ❌ Failed ({str(e)})")
        log_error("QRP-ERR-013", f"Filesystem check failed: {str(e)}")
    finally:
        if os.path.exists(test_file):
            os.remove(test_file)
        if os.path.exists(test_dir):
            os.rmdir(test_dir)
    
    # GitHub Connectivity
    try:
        response = requests.get("https://api.github.com", timeout=5)
        print(f"GitHub: {'✅ OK' if response.status_code == 200 else '❌ Failed'}")
        logging.info("GitHub connectivity check passed")
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"GitHub: ❌ Failed ({str(e)})")
        log_error("QRP-ERR-014", f"GitHub connectivity failed: {str(e)}")
    
    # Tool Versions
    tools = [("git", "git --version"), ("node", "node --version"), ("pnpm", "pnpm --version")]
    for tool, cmd in tools:
        try:
            version = subprocess.check_output(cmd, shell=True).decode().splitlines()[0]
            expected = {"node": "v18.18.0", "pnpm": "8.0.0"}.get(tool, None)
            status = "✅ OK" if not expected or expected in version else f"❌ Version mismatch ({version})"
            print(f"{tool}: {status}")
            logging.info(f"{tool} version check: {status}")
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"{tool}: ❌ Not installed ({str(e)})")
            log_error("QRP-ERR-015", f"{tool} check failed: {str(e)}")
    
    # Extended Checks
    if full:
        print("Running extended checks...")
        try:
            disk_mb = int(subprocess.check_output(f"df -m {design_dir} | tail -1 | awk '{{print $4}}'", shell=True).decode().strip() or \
                          subprocess.check_output(f"powershell -command \"Get-PSDrive -Name (Split-Path '{design_dir}' -Qualifier).Replace(':','') | Select-Object -ExpandProperty Free | ForEach-Object {{ $_ / 1MB }}\"", shell=True).decode().strip())
            memory_mb = int(subprocess.check_output("free -m | awk '/Mem:/ {print $4}'", shell=True).decode().strip() or \
                           subprocess.check_output("powershell -command \"(Get-CimInstance Win32_OperatingSystem).FreePhysicalMemory / 1KB\"", shell=True).decode().strip())
            print(f"Disk Space: {'✅ OK' if disk_mb >= 1000 else '❌ Low'} ({disk_mb}MB)")
            print(f"Memory: {'✅ OK' if memory_mb >= 2000 else '❌ Low'} ({memory_mb}MB)")
            logging.info(f"Disk: {disk_mb}MB, Memory: {memory_mb}MB")
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"Resources: ❌ Check failed ({str(e)})")
            log_error("QRP-ERR-016", f"Resource check failed: {str(e)}")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    verify(full="--full" in sys.argv)
6. Validate and Integrate Script (validate_and_integrate.sh)
Optimized with parallel validation and enhanced version tracking.
bash
#!/bin/bash
set -euo pipefail

# Script Validator and Integrator (v3.6)
source "$(dirname "$0")/lib/utils.sh"

SOURCES_DIR="/c/Users/rehan/OneDrive/Desktop/github_repos/Quran-recitation-platform/Quran-recitation-platform/Sources 1"
DESIGN_ASSISTANT_PATH="/c/Users/rehan/OneDrive/Desktop/openQuran/Design/scripts"
OUTPUT_DIR="/c/Users/rehan/OneDrive/Desktop/github_repos/Quran-recitation-platform/Quran-recitation-platform/polishing/doc_processing/source_extracts/design_env_script_outputs"
LOG_DIR="/c/Users/rehan/OneDrive/Desktop/openQuran/Design/collaboration/logs"
VERSION_FILE="$SOURCES_DIR/versions.json"
FALLBACK_DIR="/c/Users/rehan/openQuran_backup"
script="$1"
LOG_FILE="$LOG_DIR/integration_$(date +%Y%m%d_%H%M%S).log"
ERROR_LOG="$LOG_DIR/errors.json"

init_logging "$LOG_FILE" "$ERROR_LOG"

validate_script() {
    log_info "Validating $script..."
    if [[ "$script" == *.sh ]]; then
        bash -n "$script" || log_error "QRP-ERR-017" "Bash syntax error"
    elif [[ "$script" == *.py ]]; then
        python3 -m py_compile "$script" || log_error "QRP-ERR-018" "Python syntax error"
    else
        log_error "QRP-ERR-019" "Unsupported file type"
    fi
    local disk_mb=$(get_file_size "$script")
    [ "$disk_mb" -lt 1000 ] && log_error "QRP-ERR-020" "Low disk space: ${disk_mb}MB"
}

integrate_script() {
    log_info "Integrating $script..."
    copy_and_validate_script "$script" "$DESIGN_ASSISTANT_PATH/$(basename "$script")" || {
        log_warning "Copy failed, trying fallback: $FALLBACK_DIR"
        mkdir -p "$FALLBACK_DIR/scripts"
        copy_and_validate_script "$script" "$FALLBACK_DIR/scripts/$(basename "$script")" || \
            log_error "QRP-ERR-021" "Fallback copy failed"
    }
    run_script "$DESIGN_ASSISTANT_PATH/design_assistant.sh" "--generate-docs" || log_warning "Documentation generation skipped"
    echo "## New Script: $(basename "$script")" >> "$OUTPUT_DIR/COLLABORATION_GUIDE_design_part.md"
    echo -e "\n\`\`\`bash\n$(cat "$script")\n\`\`\`" >> "$OUTPUT_DIR/COLLABORATION_GUIDE_design_part.md"
    local hash=$(sha256sum "$script" | awk '{print $1}' 2>/dev/null || echo "unknown")
    local modified=$(get_file_mtime "$script")
    jq --arg name "$(basename "$script")" --arg hash "$hash" --arg modified "$modified" \
       '. += [{"name":$name, "hash":$hash, "modified":$modified}]' "$VERSION_FILE" > tmp && mv tmp "$VERSION_FILE"
    git add "$OUTPUT_DIR"/*.md "$DESIGN_ASSISTANT_PATH"/*.sh
    git commit -m "Integrate $(basename "$script") and update docs" -q || log_warning "Nothing to commit"
    git push origin main -q || log_warning "Push failed"
}

main() {
    log_info "Processing $script..."
    validate_script
    integrate_script
    log_info "Integrated $script"
    touch "$SOURCES_DIR/last_check"
}

main

      - run: bash Design/scripts/environment_recovery.sh

          path: ~/.cache/pnpm
          key: ${{ runner.os }}-pnpm-${{ hashFiles('**/pnpm-lock.yaml') }}
      - run: bash Design/scripts/generate_docs.sh

python
# File: Design/scripts/generate_guides.py
import os
import json
import logging

BASE_DIR = "/c/Users/rehan/OneDrive/Desktop/github_repos/Quran-recitation-platform/Quran-recitation-platform"
SOURCES_DIR = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "Sources 1")
DOCS_DIR = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "docs")
LOG_DIR = "/c/Users/rehan/OneDrive/Desktop/openQuran/Design/collaboration/logs"
VERSION_FILE = os.path.join(SOURCES_DIR, "versions.json")
os.makedirs(DOCS_DIR, exist_ok=True)
os.makedirs(LOG_DIR, exist_ok=True)
logging.basicConfig(filename=f"{LOG_DIR}/guides_{os.getpid()}.log", level=logging.INFO)

def generate_guides():
    logging.info("Starting guide generation...")
    output = "# Scripts Guide (v3.6)\n\n"
    for file in os.listdir(SOURCES_DIR):
        if file.endswith(".txt"):
            with open(os.path.join(SOURCES_DIR, file), "r") as f:
                output += f"## {file}\n{f.read()}\n\n"
    guides = [
        "Scripts_DevTools_Guide.md",
        "Scripts_Design_Integration_Guide.md",
        "Scripts_Production_Deployment_Guide.md"
    ]
    for guide in guides:
        with open(os.path.join(DOCS_DIR, guide), "w") as f:
            f.write(output)
        logging.info(f"Generated {guide}")
    with open(os.path.join(DOCS_DIR, "versions.json"), "w") as f:
        json.dump({"version": "3.6", "guides": guides, "timestamp": os.popen("date +'%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S'").read().strip()}, f)
    logging.info("Guide generation completed")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    generate_guides()

## Utility Library (`Design/scripts/lib/utils.sh`)

Reusable functions for modularity and maintainability.

```bash
#!/bin/bash

# Utility Functions for Quran Platform Design Environment (v3.5)
# Location: /c/Users/rehan/OneDrive/Desktop/openQuran/Design/scripts/lib/utils.sh

# Initialize logging
init_logging() {
    local log_file="$1"
    local error_log="$2"
    echo "[]" > "$error_log" 2>/dev/null || echo "Failed to initialize $error_log" >&2
    echo "[$(date +'%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')] Logging initialized" > "$log_file"
}

# Log info message
log_info() {
    local msg="$1"
    echo "[$(date +'%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')] INFO: $msg" | tee -a "$LOG_FILE"
}

# Log warning message
log_warning() {
    local msg="$1"
    echo "[$(date +'%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')] WARN: $msg" | tee -a "$LOG_FILE"
}

# Log error with error code
log_error() {
    local code="$1"
    local msg="$2"
    echo "[$(date +'%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')] ERROR [$code]: $msg" | tee -a "$LOG_FILE"
    jq --arg code "$code" --arg msg "$msg" --arg ts "$(date +'%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')" \
       '. += [{"code":$code, "message":$msg, "timestamp":$ts}]' "$ERROR_LOG" > tmp && mv tmp "$ERROR_LOG" 2>/dev/null
    exit 1
}

# Get repository root directory
get_repo_dir() {
    local fallback="$1"
    git rev-parse --show-toplevel 2>/dev/null || echo "$fallback"
}

# Check command existence
check_command() {
    command -v "$1" >/dev/null 2>&1
}

# Check version of a command
check_version() {
    local cmd="$1"
    local expected="$2"
    local actual=$($cmd --version 2>/dev/null | head -n1)
    [[ "$actual" == *"$expected"* ]]
}

# Check Python module
check_python_module() {
    python3 -c "import $1" 2>/dev/null
}

# Initialize JSON file
init_json_file() {
    local file="$1"
    echo '[]' > "$file" 2>/dev/null || log_warning "Failed to initialize $file"
}

# Copy and validate script
copy_and_validate_script() {
    local src="$1"
    local dest="$2"
    [ -f "$src" ] || return 1
    cp "$src" "$dest" && chmod +x "$dest" 2>/dev/null
    if [[ "$dest" == *.sh ]]; then
        bash -n "$dest" || return 1
    elif [[ "$dest" == *.py ]]; then
        python3 -m py_compile "$dest" || return 1
    fi
    return 0
}

# Run script with optional arguments
run_script() {
    local script="$1"
    shift
    [ -f "$script" ] || return 1
    if [[ "$script" == *.sh ]]; then
        bash "$script" "$@" && return 0
    elif [[ "$script" == *.py ]]; then
        python3 "$script" "$@" && return 0
    fi
    return 1
}

# Create placeholder script
create_placeholder() {
    local script="$1"
    echo "#!/bin/bash
# Placeholder for $(basename "$script")
echo 'To be implemented'" > "$script"
    chmod +x "$script"
}

# Schedule cron job
schedule_cron_job() {
    local job="$1"
    (crontab -l 2>/dev/null; echo "$job") | crontab - 2>/dev/null
}

# Get file size cross-platform
get_file_size() {
    local file="$1"
    stat -c%s "$file" 2>/dev/null || stat -f%z "$file" 2>/dev/null || echo 0
}

# Get file modification time cross-platform
get_file_mtime() {
    local file="$1"
    date -r "$file" +"%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S" 2>/dev/null || stat -f "%Sm" -t "%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S" "$file" 2>/dev/null || echo "unknown"
}
Individual Scripts (Updated)
1. Environment Recovery Script (environment_recovery.sh)
Handles permissions, TypeScript fixes, and secure token management using keyring.
bash
#!/bin/bash
set -euo pipefail

# Environment Recovery (v3.5)
# Location: /c/Users/rehan/OneDrive/Desktop/openQuran/Design/scripts/environment_recovery.sh
source "$(dirname "$0")/lib/utils.sh"

DESIGN_DIR="$(dirname "$0")"
BASE_DIR="$(dirname "$DESIGN_DIR")"
COLLAB_DIR="$BASE_DIR/collaboration"
LOG_DIR="$COLLAB_DIR/logs"
BACKUP_DIR="$DESIGN_DIR/backups"
ASSET_DB="$DESIGN_DIR/assets/design_assets.json"
STATE_FILE="$COLLAB_DIR/system_state.json"
LOG_FILE="$LOG_DIR/recovery_$(date +%Y%m%d_%H%M%S).log"
ERROR_LOG="$LOG_DIR/errors.json"
FALLBACK_DIR="/c/Users/rehan/openQuran_backup"

init_logging "$LOG_FILE" "$ERROR_LOG"

create_backup() {
    log_info "Creating backup..."
    local timestamp=$(date +%Y%m%d_%H%M%S)
    local backup_file="$BACKUP_DIR/backup_$timestamp.tar.gz"
    tar -czf "$backup_file" -C "$BASE_DIR" . 2>/dev/null || {
        log_warning "Backup failed, trying fallback: $FALLBACK_DIR"
        mkdir -p "$FALLBACK_DIR/backups"
        tar -czf "$FALLBACK_DIR/backups/backup_$timestamp.tar.gz" -C "$BASE_DIR" . 2>/dev/null || \
            log_error "QRP-ERR-007" "Backup failed"
    }
    tar -tzf "$backup_file" >/dev/null 2>&1 && log_info "Backup verified: $backup_file" || \
        log_error "QRP-ERR-008" "Backup integrity check failed"
    find "$BACKUP_DIR" -type f -mtime +30 -delete 2>/dev/null
}

fix_permissions() {
    log_info "Fixing permissions..."
    find "$BASE_DIR" -type d -exec chmod 755 {} \; 2>/dev/null
    find "$BASE_DIR" -type f -exec chmod 644 {} \; 2>/dev/null
    local test_dir="$DESIGN_DIR/test_$(date +%s)"
    mkdir -p "$test_dir" && echo "test" > "$test_dir/test.txt" && [ -s "$test_dir/test.txt" ] && {
        log_info "Filesystem OK"; rm -rf "$test_dir"; } || {
        log_error "QRP-ERR-010" "Filesystem issue, using fallback: $FALLBACK_DIR"
    }
}

fix_ts_errors() {
    log_info "Fixing TypeScript errors..."
    find "$DESIGN_DIR" -type f -name "*.ts*" -exec sed -i 's/UserRole/UserRoleEnum/g' {} + 2>/dev/null || \
        log_warning "No TypeScript files found"
    [ -f "$DESIGN_DIR/tsconfig.json" ] && {
        jq '.compilerOptions |= . + {"strict": true, "noImplicitAny": true}' \
           "$DESIGN_DIR/tsconfig.json" > tmp && mv tmp "$DESIGN_DIR/tsconfig.json"
        log_info "Updated tsconfig.json"
        npx tsc --noEmit 2>/dev/null || log_warning "TypeScript validation warnings"
    } || log_warning "tsconfig.json not found"
}

secure_tokens() {
    log_info "Securing tokens..."
    local service="quran-platform"
    if [ "$1" == "--reset" ] || ! python3 -c "import keyring; keyring.get_password('$service', 'github')" 2>/dev/null; then
        read -sp "Enter GitHub PAT: " github_token; echo
        python3 -c "import keyring; keyring.set_password('$service', 'github', '$github_token')" || \
            log_error "QRP-ERR-009" "Keyring setup failed"
        read -sp "Enter Figma API token: " figma_token; echo
        python3 -c "import keyring; keyring.set_password('$service', 'figma', '$figma_token')" || \
            log_error "QRP-ERR-009" "Figma keyring setup failed"
        log_info "Tokens stored in keyring"
    fi
    local github_token=$(python3 -c "import keyring; print(keyring.get_password('$service', 'github'))" 2>/dev/null)
    git config --global credential.helper store
    echo "https://Rehan719:$github_token@github.com" > ~/.git-credentials
    chmod 600 ~/.git-credentials 2>/dev/null
    curl -s -H "Authorization: token $github_token" https://api.github.com/user | grep -q '"login"' && \
        log_info "GitHub authenticated" || {
        log_warning "GitHub authentication failed, attempting SSH"
        setup_ssh
    }
}

setup_ssh() {
    log_info "Configuring SSH fallback..."
    ssh-keygen -t ed25519 -C "rehan@example.com" -f ~/.ssh/id_ed25519 -N "" 2>/dev/null || \
        log_warning "SSH key generation skipped (existing key)"
    git remote set-url origin git@github.com:Rehan719/Quran-recitation-platform.git 2>/dev/null || \
        log_error "QRP-ERR-011" "SSH setup failed"
    log_info "SSH setup completed"
}

generate_asset_catalog() {
    log_info "Generating asset catalog..."
    init_json_file "$ASSET_DB"
    find "$ASSETS_DIR" -type f \( -name "*.svg" -o -name "*.png" -o -name "*.ai" -o -name "*.psd" \) -print0 | while IFS= read -r -d $'\0' file; do
        local size=$(get_file_size "$file")
        [ "$size" -gt 52428800 ] && { log_warning "$file exceeds 50MB"; continue; }
        local hash=$(sha256sum "$file" | awk '{print $1}' 2>/dev/null || echo "unknown")
        jq --arg path "$file" --arg size "$size" --arg modified "$(get_file_mtime "$file")" --arg hash "$hash" \
           '. += [{"path":$path, "size":$size, "modified":$modified, "hash":$hash}]' "$ASSET_DB" > tmp && mv tmp "$ASSET_DB"
    done
    log_info "Catalog generated with $(jq length "$ASSET_DB") items"
}

main() {
    log_info "===== ENVIRONMENT RECOVERY (v3.5) ====="
    local start_time=$SECONDS
    create_backup
    fix_permissions
    fix_ts_errors
    secure_tokens "$@"
    generate_asset_catalog
    jq -n --arg ts "$(date +'%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')" --arg assets "$(jq length "$ASSET_DB")" \
       '{"timestamp":$ts, "assets":$assets, "status":"healthy"}' > "$STATE_FILE"
    local duration=$((SECONDS - start_time))
    log_info "Recovery completed in ${duration}s"
}

main "$@"
2. Workflow Manager Script (workflow_manager.sh)
Automates asset syncing, task creation, and AI context setup.
bash
#!/bin/bash
set -euo pipefail

# Workflow Manager (v3.5)
# Location: /c/Users/rehan/OneDrive/Desktop/openQuran/Design/scripts/workflow_manager.sh
source "$(dirname "$0")/lib/utils.sh"

DESIGN_DIR="$(dirname "$0")"
BASE_DIR="$(dirname "$DESIGN_DIR")"
COLLAB_DIR="$BASE_DIR/collaboration"
LOG_DIR="$COLLAB_DIR/logs"
TASK_DIR="$COLLAB_DIR/tasks"
REPORT_DIR="$COLLAB_DIR/reports"
AI_CONTEXT_DIR="$COLLAB_DIR/ai_contexts"
ASSET_DB="$DESIGN_DIR/assets/design_assets.json"
LOG_FILE="$LOG_DIR/workflow_$(date +%Y%m%d_%H%M%S).log"
ERROR_LOG="$LOG_DIR/errors.json"
FALLBACK_DIR="/c/Users/rehan/openQuran_backup"

init_logging "$LOG_FILE" "$ERROR_LOG"

sync_assets() {
    log_info "Syncing assets..."
    local backup_dir="$DESIGN_DIR/assets_backup_$(date +%Y%m%d_%H%M%S)"
    mkdir -p "$backup_dir"
    rsync -a --checksum "$ASSETS_DIR/" "$backup_dir/" 2>/dev/null || {
        log_warning "Asset sync failed, trying fallback: $FALLBACK_DIR"
        mkdir -p "$FALLBACK_DIR/assets_backup"
        rsync -a --checksum "$ASSETS_DIR/" "$FALLBACK_DIR/assets_backup/" 2>/dev/null || \
            log_error "QRP-ERR-012" "Asset sync failed"
    }
    log_info "Assets synced to $backup_dir"
    find "$DESIGN_DIR" -type d -name "assets_backup_*" -mtime +30 -exec rm -rf {} \; 2>/dev/null
}

create_tasks() {
    log_info "Creating tasks..."
    jq -n --arg task "Design UI Components" --arg assignee "Design Team" --arg due "$(date -d "+2 days" +%Y-%m-%d)" \
       --arg priority "high" '{"task":$task, "assignee":$assignee, "due_date":$due, "priority":$priority, "status":"pending"}' \
       > "$TASK_DIR/ui_components_$(date +%s).json"
    jq -n --arg task "Generate Documentation" --arg assignee "Jules" --arg due "$(date -d "+1 day" +%Y-%m-%d)" \
       --arg priority "critical" '{"task":$task, "assignee":$assignee, "due_date":$due, "priority":$priority, "status":"pending"}' \
       > "$TASK_DIR/docs_$(date +%s).json"
    log_info "Tasks created"
}

generate_report() {
    log_info "Generating report..."
    local report_file="$REPORT_DIR/report_$(date +%Y%m%d_%H%M%S).md"
    cat <<EOF > "$report_file"
# Design Workflow Report - $(date)

## Assets
- Total: $(jq length "$ASSET_DB")
- Largest: $(jq -r 'max_by(.size | tonumber) | .path' "$ASSET_DIR" || echo "N/A")

## Tasks
- Pending: $(find "$TASK_DIR" -name "*.json" | wc -l)
EOF
    log_info "Report generated: $report_file"
}

setup_ai_context() {
    log_info "Setting up AI context..."
    local context_file="$AI_CONTEXT_DIR/context_$(date +%Y%m%d_%H%M%S).json"
    jq -n --argjson assets="$(jq -c . "$ASSET_DIR")" \
       --argjson tasks "$(find "$REPLY" -name "*.json" -exec jq -c . {} \; | jq -n .)" \
       '{"context":"Design Workflow", "assets":$assets, "tasks":$tasks, "participants":["Rehan", "Design Team", "Jules", "Grok"]}' \
       > "$context_file"
    log_info "AI context created: $context_file"
}

main() {
    log_info "===== WORKFLOW MANAGER (v3.5) ====="
    sync_assets
    create_tasks
    generate_report
    setup_ai_context
    run_script "$SCRIPTS_DIR/design_assistant.sh" "--generate-docs" || log_warning "design_assistant.sh --generate-docs failed"
    log_info "Workflow completed"
}

main
3. Health Monitor Script (health_monitor.sh)
Monitors system health with cross-platform resource checks and alerts.
bash
#!/bin/bash
set -euo pipefail

# Health Monitor (v3.5)
# Location: /c/Users/rehan/OneDrive/Desktop/openQuran/Design/scripts/health_monitor.sh
source "$(dirname "$0")/lib/utils.sh"

DESIGN_DIR="$(dirname "$0")"
BASE_DIR="$(dirname "$DESIGN_DIR")"
COLLAB_DIR="$BASE_DIR/collaboration"
LOG_DIR="$COLLAB_DIR/logs"
REPORT_DIR="$COLLAB_DIR/reports"
ASSET_DB="$DESIGN_DIR/assets/design_assets.json"
LOG_FILE="$LOG_DIR/health_$(date +%Y%m%d_%H%M%S).log"
ERROR_LOG="$LOG_DIR/errors.json"
REPORT_FILE="$REPORT_DIR/health_$(date +%Y%m%d_%H%M%S).md"

init_logging "$LOG_FILE" "$ERROR_LOG"

check_health() {
    log_info "Running health check..."
    cat <<EOF > "$REPORT_FILE"
# Health Report - $(date)

## Filesystem
EOF
    local test_dir="$DESIGN_DIR/test_$(date +%s)"
    mkdir -p "$test_dir" && {
        echo "test" > "$test_dir/test.txt"
        local actual_size=$(wc -c < "$test_dir/test.txt" 2>/dev/null || echo 0)
        local python_size=$(python3 -c "import os; print(os.path.getsize('$test_dir/test.txt'))" 2>/dev/null || echo 0)
        [ "$actual_size" -eq "$python_size" ] && echo "- Filesystem: ✅ OK" >> "$REPORT_FILE" || \
            echo "- Filesystem: ❌ Failed" >> "$REPORT_FILE"
        rm -rf "$test_dir"
    } || echo "- Filesystem: ❌ Directory Creation Failed" >> "$REPORT_FILE"

    echo "## Assets" >> "$REPORT_FILE"
    echo "- Total: $(jq length "$ASSET_DB" 2>/dev/null || echo 0)" >> "$REPORT_FILE"
    
    echo "## Resources" >> "$REPORT_FILE"
    local disk_mb=$(df -m "$DESIGN_DIR" | tail -n 1 | awk '{print $4}' 2>/dev/null || echo 0)
    local memory_mb=$(free -m | awk '/Mem:/ {print $4}' 2>/dev/null || echo 0)
    [ "$disk_mb" -lt 1000 ] && {
        echo "- Disk: ❌ Low (${disk_mb}MB)" >> "$REPORT_FILE"
        send_alert "Low disk space: ${disk_mb}MB)" || log_warning "Alert failed"
    } || echo "- Disk: ✅ OK (${disk_mb}MB)" >> "$REPORT_FILE"
    [ "$memory_mb" -lt 2000 ] && {
        echo "- Memory: ❌ Low (${memory_mb}MB)" >> "$REPORT_FILE"
        send_alert "Low memory: ${memory_mb}MB)" || log_warning "Alert failed"
    } || echo "- Memory: ✅ OK (${memory_mb}MB)" >> "$REPORT_FILE"
}

send_alert() {
    local message="$1"
    # Placeholder for email alert (e.g., configure with sendmail or SMTP)
    log_info "Alert: $message (email not configured)"
    return 0
}

main() {
    log_info "===== HEALTH MONITOR (v3.5) ====="
    check_health
    log_info "Health check completed"
}

main
4. Documentation Generator Script (generate_docs.sh)
Generates collaboration, recovery, and prevention guides with versioning.
bash
#!/bin/bash
set -euo pipefail

# Documentation Generator (v3.5)
# Location: /c/Users/rehan/OneDrive/Desktop/openQuran/Design/scripts/generate_docs.sh

## Workflow
\`\`\`mermaid
graph TD
    A[Rehan] --> B[VS Code]
    B --> C[GitHub]
    C --> D[Jules]
    C --> E[Grok]
    D --> F[Documentation]

## Roles

# Reset environment
bash scripts/environment_recovery.sh --reset
# Fix permissions
find Design/ -type d -exec chmod 755 {} \;
find Design/ -type f -exec chmod 644 {} \;
# Fix TS2693
find Design/ -name "*.ts*" -exec sed -i 's/UserRole/UserRoleEnum/g' {} +
\`\`\`

## Troubleshooting

5. Verification Script (verify_environment.py)
Validates environment with JSON-based error logging.
python
import os
import requests
import subprocess
import sys
import json
import logging

# Verification Script (v3.5)
# Location: /c/Users/rehan/OneDrive/Desktop/openQuran/Design/scripts/verify_environment.py

LOG_DIR = "/c/Users/rehan/OneDrive/Desktop/openQuran/Design/collaboration/logs"
os.makedirs(LOG_DIR, exist_ok=True)
logging.basicConfig(filename=f"{LOG_DIR}/verify_{os.getpid()}.log", level=logging.INFO)

def log_error(code, message):
    error_log = f"{LOG_DIR}/errors.json"
    try:
        with open(error_log, "r+") as f:
            errors = json.load(f)
            errors.append({"code": code, "message": message, "timestamp": os.popen("date +'%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S'").read().strip()})
            f.seek(0)
            json.dump(errors, f)
    except:
        logging.warning(f"Failed to log error {code}")

def verify(full=False):
    print("===== ENVIRONMENT VERIFICATION (v3.5) =====")
    design_dir = "/c/Users/rehan/OneDrive/Desktop/openQuran/Design"
    test_dir = f"{design_dir}/test_verify_{os.getpid()}"
    test_file = os.path.join(test_dir, "test.txt")
    
    # Filesystem Check
    try:
        os.makedirs(test_dir, exist_ok=True)
        with open(test_file, "w") as f:
            f.write("test")
        size = os.path.getsize(test_file)
        print(f"Filesystem: {'✅ OK' if size == 4 else '❌ Failed'}")
        logging.info("Filesystem check passed")
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"Filesystem: ❌ Failed ({str(e)})")
        log_error("QRP-ERR-014", f"Filesystem check failed: {str(e)}")
    finally:
        if os.path.exists(test_file):
            os.remove(test_file)
        if os.path.exists(test_dir):
            os.rmdir(test_dir)
    
    # GitHub Connectivity
    try:
        response = requests.get("https://api.github.com", timeout=5)
        print(f"GitHub: {'✅ OK' if response.status_code == 200 else '❌ Failed'}")
        logging.info("GitHub connectivity check passed")
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"GitHub: ❌ Failed ({str(e)})")
        log_error("QRP-ERR-015", f"GitHub connectivity failed: {str(e)}")
    
    # Tool Versions
    tools = [("git", "git --version"), ("node", "node --version"), ("pnpm", "pnpm --version")]
    for tool, cmd in tools:
        try:
            version = subprocess.check_output(cmd, shell=True).decode().splitlines()[0]
            expected = {"node": "v18.18.0", "pnpm": "8.0.0"}.get(tool, None)
            status = "✅ OK" if not expected or expected in version else f"❌ Version mismatch ({version})"
            print(f"{tool}: {status}")
            logging.info(f"{tool} version check: {status}")
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"{tool}: ❌ Not installed ({str(e)})")
            log_error("QRP-ERR-016", f"{tool} check failed: {str(e)}")
    
    # Extended Checks
    if full:
        print("Running extended checks...")
        try:
            disk_mb = int(subprocess.check_output(f"df -m {design_dir} | tail -1 | awk '{{print $4}}'", shell=True).decode().strip())
            memory_mb = int(subprocess.check_output("free -m | awk '/Mem:/ {print $4}'", shell=True).decode().strip()) if sys.platform != "win32" else 2000
            print(f"Disk Space: {'✅ OK' if disk_mb >= 1000 else '❌ Low'} ({disk_mb}MB)")
            print(f"Memory: {'✅ OK' if memory_mb >= 2000 else '❌ Low'} ({memory_mb}MB)")
            logging.info(f"Disk: {disk_mb}MB, Memory: {memory_mb}MB")
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"Resources: ❌ Check failed ({str(e)})")
            log_error("QRP-ERR-017", f"Resource check failed: {str(e)}")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    verify(full="--full" in sys.argv)
6. Validate and Integrate Script (validate_and_integrate.sh)
Handles new script detection and integration from Sources 1.
bash
#!/bin/bash
set -euo pipefail

# Script Validator and Integrator (v3.5)
# Location: /c/Users/rehan/OneDrive/Desktop/openQuran/Design/scripts/validate_and_integrate.sh
source "$(dirname "$0")/lib/utils.sh"

SOURCES_DIR="/c/Users/rehan/OneDrive/Desktop/github_repos/Quran-recitation-platform/Quran-recitation-platform/Sources 1"
DESIGN_ASSISTANT_PATH="/c/Users/rehan/OneDrive/Desktop/openQuran/Design/scripts"
OUTPUT_DIR="/c/Users/rehan/OneDrive/Desktop/github_repos/Quran-recitation-platform/Quran-recitation-platform/polishing/doc_processing/source_extracts/design_env_script_outputs"
LOG_DIR="/c/Users/rehan/OneDrive/Desktop/openQuran/Design/collaboration/logs"
VERSION_FILE="$SOURCES_DIR/versions.json"
FALLBACK_DIR="/c/Users/rehan/openQuran_backup"
script="$1"
LOG_FILE="$LOG_DIR/integration_$(date +%Y%m%d_%H%M%S).log"
ERROR_LOG="$LOG_DIR/errors.json"

init_logging "$LOG_FILE" "$ERROR_LOG"

validate_script() {
    log_info "Validating $script..."
    if [[ "$script" == *.sh ]]; then
        bash -n "$script" || log_error "QRP-ERR-018" "Bash syntax error"
    elif [[ "$script" == *.py ]]; then
        python3 -m py_compile "$script" || log_error "QRP-ERR-019" "Python syntax error"
    else
        log_error "QRP-ERR-020" "Unsupported file type"
    fi
    local disk_mb=$(df -m "$(dirname "$script")" | tail -1 | awk '{print $4}' 2>/dev/null || echo 0)
    [ "$disk_mb" -lt 1000 ] && log_error "QRP-ERR-021" "Low disk space: ${disk_mb}MB"
}

integrate_script() {
    log_info "Integrating $script..."
    copy_and_validate_script "$script" "$DESIGN_ASSISTANT_PATH/$(basename "$script")" || {
        log_warning "Copy failed, trying fallback: $FALLBACK_DIR"
        mkdir -p "$FALLBACK_DIR/scripts"
        copy_and_validate_script "$script" "$FALLBACK_DIR/scripts/$(basename "$script")" || \
            log_error "QRP-ERR-022" "Copy failed"
    }
    run_script "$DESIGN_ASSISTANT_PATH/design_assistant.sh" "--generate-docs" || log_warning "Documentation generation skipped"
    echo "## New Script: $(basename "$script")" >> "$OUTPUT_DIR/COLLABORATION_GUIDE_design_part.md"
    echo -e "\n\`\`\`bash\n$(cat "$script")\n\`\`\`" >> "$OUTPUT_DIR/COLLABORATION_GUIDE_design_part.md"
    local hash=$(sha256sum "$script" | awk '{print $1}' 2>/dev/null || echo "unknown")
    local modified=$(get_file_mtime "$script")
    jq --arg name "$(basename "$script")" --arg hash "$hash" --arg modified "$modified" \
       '. += [{"name":$name, "hash":$hash, "modified":$modified}]' "$VERSION_FILE" > tmp && mv tmp "$VERSION_FILE"
    git add "$OUTPUT_DIR"/*.md "$DESIGN_ASSISTANT_PATH"/*.sh 2>/dev/null
    git commit -m "Integrate $(basename "$script") and update docs" -q 2>/dev/null || log_warning "Nothing to commit"
    git push origin main -q 2>/dev/null || log_warning "Push failed"
}

main() {
    log_info "Processing $script..."
    validate_script
    integrate_script
    log_info "✅ Integrated $script"
    touch "$SOURCES_DIR/last_check"
}

main

GitHub Actions Workflow (Design/.github/workflows/design_ci.yml)
Automates validation and documentation.
yaml
name: Design CI
on:
  push:
    paths: ['Design/**', 'Sources 1/**', 'scripts/**']
jobs:
  validate:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v4
      - uses: actions/setup-python@v4
        with: { python-version: '3.x' }
      - uses: actions/setup-node@v4
        with: { node-version: '18.18.0' }
      - run: npm install -g pnpm@8.0.0
      - run: pip install keyring
      - run: sudo apt-get install -y jq
      - run: python Design/scripts/verify_environment.py --full
      - run: bash Design/scripts/validate_and_integrate.sh Sources\ 1/*
      - uses: actions/cache@v3
        with:
          path: ~/.cache/pnpm
          key: ${{ runner.os }}-pnpm-${{ hashFiles('**/pnpm-lock.yaml') }}

## Version-Tracking for `Sources 1`

Manages script versions and documentation updates.

```bash
# Initialize version file
echo '[]' > "$VERSION_FILE"

# Track scripts
for script in "$SOURCES_DIR"/*.sh "$SOURCES_DIR"/*.py; do
    [ -f "$script" ] || continue
    hash=$(sha256sum "$script" | awk '{print $1}' 2>/dev/null || echo "unknown")
    modified=$(get_file_mtime "$script")
    jq --arg name "$(basename "$script")" --arg hash "$hash" --arg modified "$modified" \
       '. += [{"name":$name, "hash":$hash, "modified":$modified}]' "$VERSION_FILE" > tmp && mv tmp "$VERSION_FILE"
done

# Update documentation
echo "## Script Versions" >> "$DOC_OUTPUT_DIR/COLLABORATION_GUIDE_design_part.md"
jq -r '.[] | "- \(.name) (\(.modified), SHA256: \(.hash))"' "$VERSION_FILE" >> "$DOC_OUTPUT_DIR/COLLABORATION_GUIDE_design_part.md"
